(**********************************************************************************

 Structured cospans

 In this file, we define the 2-sided displayed category of structured cospans. Our
 definition is based on Theorem 3.1 in Structured Versus Decorated Cospans by Baez,
 Courser, and Vasilakopoulou. Note that even though they define a monoidal double
 category, the definition in this file only consists of the horizontal and vertical
 morphisms, and the squares. For that reason, we don't need to assume the existence
 of pushouts in any of the involved categories and we also don't need to assume
 that the functor `L` preserves pushouts, We also prove that the obtained 2-sided
 displayed category is univalent.

 Fix categories `A` and `X` and a functor `A ⟶ X`. The construction of the 2-sided
 displayed category is done in multiple steps. In this 2-sided displayed category,
 the objects describe what a structured cospan between objects `a` and `b` in `A`.
 Such a cospan consists of an object `x` in `X` and morphisms `L a --> x` and
 `L b --> x`. Each part of this definition is put in its own 2-sided displayed
 category:
 - We add the object `x` in [struct_cospans_ob]
 - The morphism `L a --> x` is added in [struct_cospans_mor_left], which is a
   displayed category on the total category of [struct_cospans_ob].
 - The morphism `L b --> x` is added in [struct_cospans_mor_right], which is a
   displayed category on the total category of [struct_cospans_ob].
 Combining these together by taking products and a sigma, we obtain the 2-sided
 displayed category of structured cospans.

 We also characterize global isomorphism squares (i.e., those squares of which the
 vertical sides are identities) of structured cospans. In addition, we give some
 standard structured cospans. Furthermore, we define an action of functors on
 structured cospans, and we show that this gives rise to a functor between
 2-sided displayed categories.

 Contents
 1. The 2-sided displayed category of structured cospans
 2. Builders and accessors for structured cospans
 3. The univalence of the 2-sided displayed category of structured cospans
 4. Isos of structured cospans
 5. The identity structured cospans
 6. The composition of structured cospans
 7. The left unitor of structured cospans
 8. The right unitor of structured cospans
 9. The associator of structured cospans
 10. Companions and conjoints
 11. Functors on structured cospans

 **********************************************************************************)

Local Open Scope cat.

Section StructuredCospans.
  Context {A X : category}
          (L : A ⟶ X).

  (** * 1. The 2-sided displayed category of structured cospans *)
  Definition struct_cospans_ob
    : twosided_disp_cat A A
    := constant_twosided_disp_cat A A X.

  
A, X: category
L: A ⟶ X
disp_cat_ob_mor
  (total_twosided_disp_category struct_cospans_ob)

  
A, X: category
L: A ⟶ X
disp_cat_ob_mor
  (total_twosided_disp_category struct_cospans_ob)

    
A, X: category
L: A ⟶ X
total_twosided_disp_category struct_cospans_ob → UU
A, X: category
L: A ⟶ X
(λ obd : total_twosided_disp_category
           struct_cospans_ob → UU,
 ∏
 x y : total_twosided_disp_category struct_cospans_ob,
 obd x
 → obd y
   → total_twosided_disp_category struct_cospans_ob
     ⟦ x, y ⟧ → UU) ?pr1

    
A, X: category
L: A ⟶ X
total_twosided_disp_category struct_cospans_ob → UU
 exact (λ xyz, L (pr1 xyz) --> pr22 xyz).
    
A, X: category
L: A ⟶ X
(λ obd : total_twosided_disp_category
           struct_cospans_ob → UU,
 ∏
 x y : total_twosided_disp_category struct_cospans_ob,
 obd x
 → obd y
   → total_twosided_disp_category struct_cospans_ob
     ⟦ x, y ⟧ → UU)
  (λ xyz : total_twosided_disp_category
             struct_cospans_ob,
   X ⟦ L (pr1 xyz), pr22 xyz ⟧)
 exact (λ xyz₁ xyz₂ l₁ l₂ fgh,
             l₁ · pr22 fgh
             =
             #L (pr1 fgh) · l₂).
  Defined.

A, X: category
L: A ⟶ X
xyz₁, xyz₂, xyz₃: ∑ _ _ : A, X
fgh₁: ∑ (_ : A ⟦ pr1 xyz₁, pr1 xyz₂ ⟧)
(_ : A ⟦ pr12 xyz₁, pr12 xyz₂ ⟧),
X ⟦ pr22 xyz₁, pr22 xyz₂ ⟧
fgh₂: ∑ (_ : A ⟦ pr1 xyz₂, pr1 xyz₃ ⟧)
(_ : A ⟦ pr12 xyz₂, pr12 xyz₃ ⟧),
X ⟦ pr22 xyz₂, pr22 xyz₃ ⟧
h₁: X ⟦ L (pr1 xyz₁), pr22 xyz₁ ⟧
h₂: X ⟦ L (pr1 xyz₂), pr22 xyz₂ ⟧
h₃: X ⟦ L (pr1 xyz₃), pr22 xyz₃ ⟧
p₁: h₁ · pr22 fgh₁ = # L (pr1 fgh₁) · h₂
p₂: h₂ · pr22 fgh₂ = # L (pr1 fgh₂) · h₃
h₁ · (pr22 fgh₁ · pr22 fgh₂) =
# L (pr1 fgh₁ · pr1 fgh₂) · h₃

isaprop (xx -->[ f] yy)

      apply homset_property.
  Qed.

  Definition struct_cospans_mors
    : disp_cat (total_twosided_disp_category struct_cospans_ob)
    := dirprod_disp_cat
         struct_cospans_mor_left
         struct_cospans_mor_right.

  Definition twosided_disp_cat_of_struct_cospans
    : twosided_disp_cat A A
    := sigma_twosided_disp_cat _ struct_cospans_mors.

  (** * 2. Builders and accessors for structured cospans *)
  Definition struct_cospan
             (a b : A)
    : UU
    := twosided_disp_cat_of_struct_cospans a b.

  Definition make_struct_cospan
             {a b : A}
             (x : X)
             (l : L a --> x)
             (r : L b --> x)
    : struct_cospan a b
    :=  x ,, l ,, r.

  Definition ob_of_struct_cospan
             {a b : A}
             (s : struct_cospan a b)
    : X
    := pr1 s.

  Definition mor_left_of_struct_cospan
             {a b : A}
             (s : struct_cospan a b)
    : L a --> ob_of_struct_cospan s
    := pr12 s.

  Definition mor_right_of_struct_cospan
             {a b : A}
             (s : struct_cospan a b)
    : L b --> ob_of_struct_cospan s
    := pr22 s.

  Definition struct_cospan_sqr
             {a₁ a₂ b₁ b₂ : A}
             (f : a₁ --> a₂)
             (g : b₁ --> b₂)
             (s₁ : struct_cospan a₁ b₁)
             (s₂ : struct_cospan a₂ b₂)
    : UU
    := s₁ -->[ f ][ g ] s₂.

  Definition struct_cospan_laws
             {a₁ a₂ b₁ b₂ : A}
             (f : a₁ --> a₂)
             (g : b₁ --> b₂)
             (s₁ : struct_cospan a₁ b₁)
             (s₂ : struct_cospan a₂ b₂)
             (φ : ob_of_struct_cospan s₁ --> ob_of_struct_cospan s₂)
    : UU
    := (mor_left_of_struct_cospan s₁ · φ
        =
        #L f · mor_left_of_struct_cospan s₂)
       ×
       (mor_right_of_struct_cospan s₁ · φ
        =
        #L g · mor_right_of_struct_cospan s₂).

  Definition make_struct_cospan_sqr
             {a₁ a₂ b₁ b₂ : A}
             {f : a₁ --> a₂}
             {g : b₁ --> b₂}
             {s₁ : struct_cospan a₁ b₁}
             {s₂ : struct_cospan a₂ b₂}
             (φ : ob_of_struct_cospan s₁ --> ob_of_struct_cospan s₂)
             (Hφ : struct_cospan_laws f g _ _ φ)
    : struct_cospan_sqr f g s₁ s₂
    := φ ,, pr1 Hφ ,, pr2 Hφ.

  Definition struct_cospan_sqr_ob_mor
             {a₁ a₂ b₁ b₂ : A}
             {f : a₁ --> a₂}
             {g : b₁ --> b₂}
             {s₁ : struct_cospan a₁ b₁}
             {s₂ : struct_cospan a₂ b₂}
             (sq : struct_cospan_sqr f g s₁ s₂)
    : ob_of_struct_cospan s₁ --> ob_of_struct_cospan s₂
    := pr1 sq.

  
A, X: category
L: A ⟶ X
a₁, a₂, b₁, b₂: A
f: A ⟦ a₁, a₂ ⟧
g: A ⟦ b₁, b₂ ⟧
s₁: struct_cospan a₁ b₁
s₂: struct_cospan a₂ b₂
sq: struct_cospan_sqr f g s₁ s₂
mor_left_of_struct_cospan s₁
· struct_cospan_sqr_ob_mor sq =
# L f · mor_left_of_struct_cospan s₂

  
A, X: category
L: A ⟶ X
a₁, a₂, b₁, b₂: A
f: A ⟦ a₁, a₂ ⟧
g: A ⟦ b₁, b₂ ⟧
s₁: struct_cospan a₁ b₁
s₂: struct_cospan a₂ b₂
sq: struct_cospan_sqr f g s₁ s₂
mor_left_of_struct_cospan s₁
· struct_cospan_sqr_ob_mor sq =
# L f · mor_left_of_struct_cospan s₂

    exact (pr12 sq).
  Qed.

  (** * 4. Isos of structured cospans *)
  
A, X: category
L: A ⟶ X
a₁, a₂, b₁, b₂: A
f, f': A ⟦ a₁, a₂ ⟧
p: f = f'
g, g': A ⟦ b₁, b₂ ⟧
q: g = g'
s₁: struct_cospan a₁ b₁
s₂: struct_cospan a₂ b₂
sq: struct_cospan_sqr f g s₁ s₂
struct_cospan_sqr_ob_mor (trf₂ sq) =
struct_cospan_sqr_ob_mor sq

Section StandardCospans.
  Context {A X : category}
          (L : A ⟶ X).

  (** * 5. The identity structured cospans *)
  
A, X: category
L: A ⟶ X
a: A
struct_cospan L a a

L: A ⟶ X
a: A
struct_cospan L a a

a: A

L: A ⟶ X

X
 exact (L a).

 exact (identity _).
  Defined.

  
A, X: category
L: A ⟶ X
x, y: A
f: A ⟦ x, y ⟧
struct_cospan_laws L f f (id_struct_cospan x)
  (id_struct_cospan y) (# L f)

  
A, X: category
L: A ⟶ X
x, y: A
f: A ⟦ x, y ⟧
struct_cospan_laws L f f (id_struct_cospan x)
  (id_struct_cospan y) (# L f)

    
A, X: category
L: A ⟶ X
x, y: A
f: A ⟦ x, y ⟧
identity (L x) · # L f = # L f · identity (L y)
A, X: category
L: A ⟶ X
x, y: A
f: A ⟦ x, y ⟧
identity (L x) · # L f = # L f · identity (L y)

    
A, X: category
L: A ⟶ X
x, y: A
f: A ⟦ x, y ⟧
identity (L x) · # L f = # L f · identity (L y)
 
A, X: category
L: A ⟶ X
x, y: A
f: A ⟦ x, y ⟧
# L f = # L f

      apply idpath.
    
A, X: category
L: A ⟶ X
x, y: A
f: A ⟦ x, y ⟧
identity (L x) · # L f = # L f · identity (L y)
 
A, X: category
L: A ⟶ X
x, y: A
f: A ⟦ x, y ⟧
# L f = # L f

      apply idpath.
  Qed.

  (id_struct_cospan y)

  (id_struct_cospan y) ?φ

 exact (#L f).

  Defined.

  Context (PX : Pushouts X).

  (** * 6. The composition of structured cospans *)
  Section CompCospan.
    Context {x y z : A}
            (s : struct_cospan L x y)
            (t : struct_cospan L y z).

    Definition comp_struct_cospan_Pushout
      : Pushout (mor_right_of_struct_cospan L s) (mor_left_of_struct_cospan L t)
      := PX _ _ _ (mor_right_of_struct_cospan L s) (mor_left_of_struct_cospan L t).

L: A ⟶ X
PX: Pushouts X

t: struct_cospan L y z
struct_cospan L x z

t: struct_cospan L y z
struct_cospan L x z

x, y, z: A
s: struct_cospan L x y
t: struct_cospan L y z
X
A, X: category
L: A ⟶ X

    Defined.
  End CompCospan.

  Section CompCospanMor.
    Context {x₁ x₂ y₁ y₂ z₁ z₂ : A}
            {v₁ : x₁ --> x₂} {v₂ : y₁ --> y₂} {v₃ : z₁ --> z₂}
            {h₁ : struct_cospan L x₁ y₁}
            {h₂ : struct_cospan L y₁ z₁}
            {k₁ : struct_cospan L x₂ y₂}
            {k₂ : struct_cospan L y₂ z₂}
            (s₁ : struct_cospan_sqr L v₁ v₂ h₁ k₁)
            (s₂ : struct_cospan_sqr L v₂ v₃ h₂ k₂).

 abstract
          (rewrite !assoc ;
           rewrite struct_cospan_sqr_mor_right ;
           rewrite struct_cospan_sqr_mor_left ;
           rewrite !assoc' ;
           apply maponpaths ;
           apply PushoutSqrCommutes).
    Defined.

s₁: struct_cospan_sqr L v₁ v₂ h₁ k₁
s₂: struct_cospan_sqr L v₂ v₃ h₂ k₂
mor_right_of_struct_cospan L h₂
· PushoutIn2 (comp_struct_cospan_Pushout h₁ h₂)
· mor_of_comp_struct_cospan_mor =
# L v₃
· (mor_right_of_struct_cospan L k₂
   · PushoutIn2 (comp_struct_cospan_Pushout k₁ k₂))

    (struct_cospan_sqr_ob_mor L s₂

 exact (PushoutIn1 _ · PushoutIn2 _).

             apply idpath).

           rewrite !assoc' ;

mor_right_of_struct_cospan L h₃
· PushoutIn2 (comp_struct_cospan_Pushout h₂ h₃)
· PushoutIn2
    (comp_struct_cospan_Pushout h₁
       (comp_struct_cospan h₂ h₃))
· struct_cospan_associator_mor =
# L (identity z)
· (mor_right_of_struct_cospan L h₃
   · PushoutIn2
       (comp_struct_cospan_Pushout
          (comp_struct_cospan h₁ h₂) h₃))

      
A, X: category
L: A ⟶ X
PX: Pushouts X
w, x, y, z: A
h₁: struct_cospan L w x
h₂: struct_cospan L x y
h₃: struct_cospan L y z
mor_left_of_struct_cospan L h₁
· PushoutIn1
    (comp_struct_cospan_Pushout h₁
       (comp_struct_cospan h₂ h₃))
· struct_cospan_associator_mor =
# L (identity w)
· (mor_left_of_struct_cospan L h₁
   · PushoutIn1 (comp_struct_cospan_Pushout h₁ h₂)
   · PushoutIn1
       (comp_struct_cospan_Pushout
          (comp_struct_cospan h₁ h₂) h₃))

L: A ⟶ X
PX: Pushouts X
w, x, y, z: A
h₁: struct_cospan L w x
h₂: struct_cospan L x y
h₃: struct_cospan L y z
mor_left_of_struct_cospan L h₁
· PushoutIn1
    (comp_struct_cospan_Pushout h₁
       (comp_struct_cospan h₂ h₃))

       (PushoutIn2
          (comp_struct_cospan_Pushout
             (comp_struct_cospan h₁ h₂) h₃))
       struct_cospan_associator_mor_subproof)
    struct_cospan_associator_mor_subproof0 =

· PushoutIn1 (comp_struct_cospan_Pushout h₁ h₂)
· PushoutIn1
    (comp_struct_cospan_Pushout
       (comp_struct_cospan h₁ h₂) h₃)

A, X: category
L: A ⟶ X
PX: Pushouts X
x, y: A
f: A ⟦ x, y ⟧
X ⟦ ob_of_struct_cospan L struct_cospan_conjoint,
ob_of_struct_cospan L (id_struct_cospan y) ⟧
 apply identity.
      
A, X: category
L: A ⟶ X
PX: Pushouts X
x, y: A
f: A ⟦ x, y ⟧
struct_cospan_laws L (identity y) f
  struct_cospan_conjoint (id_struct_cospan y)
  (identity
     (ob_of_struct_cospan L (id_struct_cospan y)))
 abstract
          (split ; cbn ; [ rewrite (functor_id L) ; apply idpath | ] ;
           apply idpath).
    Defined.
  End CompanionsAndConjoints.
End StandardCospans.

(** * 11. Functors on structured cospans *)
Section FunctorOnCospans.
  Context {A₁ A₂ X₁ X₂ : category}
          {L₁ : A₁ ⟶ X₁}
          {L₂ : A₂ ⟶ X₂}
          {FA : A₁ ⟶ A₂}
          {FX : X₁ ⟶ X₂}
          (α : FA ∙ L₂ ⟹ L₁ ∙ FX).

  
A₁, A₂, X₁, X₂: category
L₁: A₁ ⟶ X₁
L₂: A₂ ⟶ X₂
FA: A₁ ⟶ A₂
FX: X₁ ⟶ X₂
α: FA ∙ L₂ ⟹ L₁ ∙ FX
x, y: A₁
f: struct_cospan L₁ x y
struct_cospan L₂ (FA x) (FA y)

  
A₁, A₂, X₁, X₂: category
L₁: A₁ ⟶ X₁
L₂: A₂ ⟶ X₂
FA: A₁ ⟶ A₂
FX: X₁ ⟶ X₂
α: FA ∙ L₂ ⟹ L₁ ∙ FX
x, y: A₁
f: struct_cospan L₁ x y
struct_cospan L₂ (FA x) (FA y)

    
A₁, A₂, X₁, X₂: category
L₁: A₁ ⟶ X₁
L₂: A₂ ⟶ X₂
FA: A₁ ⟶ A₂
FX: X₁ ⟶ X₂
α: FA ∙ L₂ ⟹ L₁ ∙ FX
x, y: A₁
f: struct_cospan L₁ x y
X₂
A₁, A₂, X₁, X₂: category
L₁: A₁ ⟶ X₁
L₂: A₂ ⟶ X₂
FA: A₁ ⟶ A₂
FX: X₁ ⟶ X₂
α: FA ∙ L₂ ⟹ L₁ ∙ FX
x, y: A₁
f: struct_cospan L₁ x y
X₂ ⟦ L₂ (FA x), ?x ⟧
A₁, A₂, X₁, X₂: category
L₁: A₁ ⟶ X₁
L₂: A₂ ⟶ X₂
FA: A₁ ⟶ A₂
FX: X₁ ⟶ X₂
α: FA ∙ L₂ ⟹ L₁ ∙ FX
x, y: A₁
f: struct_cospan L₁ x y
X₂ ⟦ L₂ (FA y), ?x ⟧

    
A₁, A₂, X₁, X₂: category
L₁: A₁ ⟶ X₁
L₂: A₂ ⟶ X₂
FA: A₁ ⟶ A₂
FX: X₁ ⟶ X₂
α: FA ∙ L₂ ⟹ L₁ ∙ FX
x, y: A₁
f: struct_cospan L₁ x y
X₂
 exact (FX (ob_of_struct_cospan _ f)).
    
A₁, A₂, X₁, X₂: category
L₁: A₁ ⟶ X₁
L₂: A₂ ⟶ X₂
FA: A₁ ⟶ A₂
FX: X₁ ⟶ X₂
α: FA ∙ L₂ ⟹ L₁ ∙ FX
x, y: A₁
f: struct_cospan L₁ x y
X₂ ⟦ L₂ (FA x), FX (ob_of_struct_cospan L₁ f) ⟧
 exact (α x · #FX (mor_left_of_struct_cospan _ f)).
    
A₁, A₂, X₁, X₂: category
L₁: A₁ ⟶ X₁
L₂: A₂ ⟶ X₂
FA: A₁ ⟶ A₂
FX: X₁ ⟶ X₂
α: FA ∙ L₂ ⟹ L₁ ∙ FX
x, y: A₁
f: struct_cospan L₁ x y
X₂ ⟦ L₂ (FA y), FX (ob_of_struct_cospan L₁ f) ⟧
 exact (α y · #FX (mor_right_of_struct_cospan _ f)).
  Defined.

  
A₁, A₂, X₁, X₂: category
L₁: A₁ ⟶ X₁
L₂: A₂ ⟶ X₂
FA: A₁ ⟶ A₂
FX: X₁ ⟶ X₂
α: FA ∙ L₂ ⟹ L₁ ∙ FX
x₁, x₂, y₁, y₂: A₁
f₁: struct_cospan L₁ x₁ y₁
f₂: struct_cospan L₁ x₂ y₂
vx: A₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
vy: A₁ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧
sq: struct_cospan_sqr L₁ vx vy f₁ f₂
struct_cospan_sqr L₂ (# FA vx) (# FA vy)
  (functor_on_struct_cospan f₁)
  (functor_on_struct_cospan f₂)

  
A₁, A₂, X₁, X₂: category
L₁: A₁ ⟶ X₁
L₂: A₂ ⟶ X₂
FA: A₁ ⟶ A₂
FX: X₁ ⟶ X₂
α: FA ∙ L₂ ⟹ L₁ ∙ FX
x₁, x₂, y₁, y₂: A₁
f₁: struct_cospan L₁ x₁ y₁
f₂: struct_cospan L₁ x₂ y₂
vx: A₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
vy: A₁ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧
sq: struct_cospan_sqr L₁ vx vy f₁ f₂
struct_cospan_sqr L₂ (# FA vx) (# FA vy)
  (functor_on_struct_cospan f₁)
  (functor_on_struct_cospan f₂)

    
A₁, A₂, X₁, X₂: category
L₁: A₁ ⟶ X₁
L₂: A₂ ⟶ X₂
FA: A₁ ⟶ A₂
FX: X₁ ⟶ X₂
α: FA ∙ L₂ ⟹ L₁ ∙ FX
x₁, x₂, y₁, y₂: A₁
f₁: struct_cospan L₁ x₁ y₁
f₂: struct_cospan L₁ x₂ y₂
vx: A₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
vy: A₁ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧
sq: struct_cospan_sqr L₁ vx vy f₁ f₂
X₂
⟦ ob_of_struct_cospan L₂ (functor_on_struct_cospan f₁),
ob_of_struct_cospan L₂ (functor_on_struct_cospan f₂) ⟧
A₁, A₂, X₁, X₂: category
L₁: A₁ ⟶ X₁
L₂: A₂ ⟶ X₂

struct_cospan_laws L₂ (# FA vx) (# FA vy)
  (functor_on_struct_cospan f₁)
  (functor_on_struct_cospan f₂) ?φ

    
A₁, A₂, X₁, X₂: category
L₁: A₁ ⟶ X₁
L₂: A₂ ⟶ X₂
FA: A₁ ⟶ A₂
FX: X₁ ⟶ X₂
α: FA ∙ L₂ ⟹ L₁ ∙ FX
x₁, x₂, y₁, y₂: A₁
f₁: struct_cospan L₁ x₁ y₁
f₂: struct_cospan L₁ x₂ y₂
vx: A₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
vy: A₁ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧
sq: struct_cospan_sqr L₁ vx vy f₁ f₂
X₂
⟦ ob_of_struct_cospan L₂ (functor_on_struct_cospan f₁),
ob_of_struct_cospan L₂ (functor_on_struct_cospan f₂) ⟧
 exact (#FX (struct_cospan_sqr_ob_mor _ sq)).
    
A₁, A₂, X₁, X₂: category
L₁: A₁ ⟶ X₁
L₂: A₂ ⟶ X₂
FA: A₁ ⟶ A₂
FX: X₁ ⟶ X₂
α: FA ∙ L₂ ⟹ L₁ ∙ FX
x₁, x₂, y₁, y₂: A₁
f₁: struct_cospan L₁ x₁ y₁
f₂: struct_cospan L₁ x₂ y₂
vx: A₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
vy: A₁ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧
sq: struct_cospan_sqr L₁ vx vy f₁ f₂
struct_cospan_laws L₂ (# FA vx) (# FA vy)
  (functor_on_struct_cospan f₁)
  (functor_on_struct_cospan f₂)
  (# FX (struct_cospan_sqr_ob_mor L₁ sq))
 abstract
        (split ; cbn ;
         [ rewrite !assoc' ;
           rewrite <- functor_comp ;
           rewrite struct_cospan_sqr_mor_left ;
           rewrite functor_comp ;
           rewrite !assoc ;
           apply maponpaths_2 ;
           exact (!(nat_trans_ax α _ _ vx))
         | rewrite !assoc' ;
           rewrite <- functor_comp ;
           rewrite struct_cospan_sqr_mor_right ;
           rewrite functor_comp ;
           rewrite !assoc ;
           apply maponpaths_2 ;
           exact (!(nat_trans_ax α _ _ vy)) ]).
  Defined.

  
A₁, A₂, X₁, X₂: category
L₁: A₁ ⟶ X₁
L₂: A₂ ⟶ X₂
FA: A₁ ⟶ A₂
FX: X₁ ⟶ X₂
α: FA ∙ L₂ ⟹ L₁ ∙ FX
twosided_disp_functor_data FA FA
  (twosided_disp_cat_of_struct_cospans L₁)
  (twosided_disp_cat_of_struct_cospans L₂)

twosided_disp_functor_data FA FA
  (twosided_disp_cat_of_struct_cospans L₁)
  (twosided_disp_cat_of_struct_cospans L₂)

    
A₁, A₂, X₁, X₂: category
L₁: A₁ ⟶ X₁
L₂: A₂ ⟶ X₂
FA: A₁ ⟶ A₂
FX: X₁ ⟶ X₂
α: FA ∙ L₂ ⟹ L₁ ∙ FX
∏ x y : A₁,
twosided_disp_cat_of_struct_cospans L₁ x y
→ twosided_disp_cat_of_struct_cospans L₂ (FA x) (FA y)
A₁, A₂, X₁, X₂: category
L₁: A₁ ⟶ X₁
L₂: A₂ ⟶ X₂
FA: A₁ ⟶ A₂
FX: X₁ ⟶ X₂
α: FA ∙ L₂ ⟹ L₁ ∙ FX
(λ FGob : ∏ x y : A₁,
          twosided_disp_cat_of_struct_cospans L₁ x y
          → twosided_disp_cat_of_struct_cospans L₂
              (FA x) (FA y),
 ∏ (x₁ x₂ y₁ y₂ : A₁)
 (xy₁ : twosided_disp_cat_of_struct_cospans L₁ x₁ y₁)
 (xy₂ : twosided_disp_cat_of_struct_cospans L₁ x₂ y₂)
 (f : A₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧) (g : A₁ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧),
 xy₁ -->[ f ][ g] xy₂
 → FGob x₁ y₁ xy₁ -->[ # FA f
   ][ # FA g] FGob x₂ y₂ xy₂) ?pr1

    
A₁, A₂, X₁, X₂: category
L₁: A₁ ⟶ X₁
L₂: A₂ ⟶ X₂
FA: A₁ ⟶ A₂
FX: X₁ ⟶ X₂
α: FA ∙ L₂ ⟹ L₁ ∙ FX
∏ x y : A₁,
twosided_disp_cat_of_struct_cospans L₁ x y
→ twosided_disp_cat_of_struct_cospans L₂ (FA x) (FA y)
 exact (λ x y f, functor_on_struct_cospan f).
    
A₁, A₂, X₁, X₂: category
L₁: A₁ ⟶ X₁
L₂: A₂ ⟶ X₂
FA: A₁ ⟶ A₂
FX: X₁ ⟶ X₂
α: FA ∙ L₂ ⟹ L₁ ∙ FX
(λ FGob : ∏ x y : A₁,
          twosided_disp_cat_of_struct_cospans L₁ x y
          → twosided_disp_cat_of_struct_cospans L₂
              (FA x) (FA y),
 ∏ (x₁ x₂ y₁ y₂ : A₁)
 (xy₁ : twosided_disp_cat_of_struct_cospans L₁ x₁ y₁)
 (xy₂ : twosided_disp_cat_of_struct_cospans L₁ x₂ y₂)
 (f : A₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧) (g : A₁ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧),
 xy₁ -->[ f ][ g] xy₂
 → FGob x₁ y₁ xy₁ -->[ # FA f
   ][ # FA g] FGob x₂ y₂ xy₂)
  (λ (x y : A₁)
   (f : twosided_disp_cat_of_struct_cospans L₁ x y),
   functor_on_struct_cospan f)
 exact (λ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ sq, functor_on_struct_cospan_sqr sq).
  Defined.

  
A₁, A₂, X₁, X₂: category
L₁: A₁ ⟶ X₁
L₂: A₂ ⟶ X₂
FA: A₁ ⟶ A₂
FX: X₁ ⟶ X₂
α: FA ∙ L₂ ⟹ L₁ ∙ FX
twosided_disp_functor_laws FA FA
  (twosided_disp_cat_of_struct_cospans L₁)
  (twosided_disp_cat_of_struct_cospans L₂)
  twosided_disp_cat_of_struct_cospans_functor_data

  (twosided_disp_cat_of_struct_cospans L₁)
  (twosided_disp_cat_of_struct_cospans L₂)
  twosided_disp_cat_of_struct_cospans_functor_data

α: FA ∙ L₂ ⟹ L₁ ∙ FX
twosided_disp_functor_id_law FA FA
  (twosided_disp_cat_of_struct_cospans L₁)
  (twosided_disp_cat_of_struct_cospans L₂)
  twosided_disp_cat_of_struct_cospans_functor_data
A₁, A₂, X₁, X₂: category
L₁: A₁ ⟶ X₁
L₂: A₂ ⟶ X₂
FA: A₁ ⟶ A₂
FX: X₁ ⟶ X₂
α: FA ∙ L₂ ⟹ L₁ ∙ FX
twosided_disp_functor_comp_law FA FA
  (twosided_disp_cat_of_struct_cospans L₁)
  (twosided_disp_cat_of_struct_cospans L₂)
  twosided_disp_cat_of_struct_cospans_functor_data

    
A₁, A₂, X₁, X₂: category
L₁: A₁ ⟶ X₁
L₂: A₂ ⟶ X₂
FA: A₁ ⟶ A₂
FX: X₁ ⟶ X₂
α: FA ∙ L₂ ⟹ L₁ ∙ FX
twosided_disp_functor_id_law FA FA
  (twosided_disp_cat_of_struct_cospans L₁)
  (twosided_disp_cat_of_struct_cospans L₂)
  twosided_disp_cat_of_struct_cospans_functor_data
 
A₁, A₂, X₁, X₂: category
L₁: A₁ ⟶ X₁
L₂: A₂ ⟶ X₂
FA: A₁ ⟶ A₂
FX: X₁ ⟶ X₂
α: FA ∙ L₂ ⟹ L₁ ∙ FX
x, y: A₁
f: twosided_disp_cat_of_struct_cospans L₁ x y
(#2 twosided_disp_cat_of_struct_cospans_functor_data)
  (id_two_disp f) =
trb₂ id_two_disp
       (twosided_disp_cat_of_struct_cospans_functor_data
          x y f)

      
A₁, A₂, X₁, X₂: category
L₁: A₁ ⟶ X₁
L₂: A₂ ⟶ X₂
FA: A₁ ⟶ A₂
FX: X₁ ⟶ X₂
α: FA ∙ L₂ ⟹ L₁ ∙ FX
x, y: A₁
f: twosided_disp_cat_of_struct_cospans L₁ x y
struct_cospan_sqr_ob_mor L₂
  ((#2 twosided_disp_cat_of_struct_cospans_functor_data)
     (id_two_disp f)) =
struct_cospan_sqr_ob_mor L₂
  (trb₂ id_two_disp
          (twosided_disp_cat_of_struct_cospans_functor_data
             x y f))

      
A₁, A₂, X₁, X₂: category
L₁: A₁ ⟶ X₁
L₂: A₂ ⟶ X₂
FA: A₁ ⟶ A₂
FX: X₁ ⟶ X₂
α: FA ∙ L₂ ⟹ L₁ ∙ FX
x, y: A₁
f: twosided_disp_cat_of_struct_cospans L₁ x y
# FX (identity (pr1 f)) =
identity (FX (ob_of_struct_cospan L₁ f))

      apply functor_id.
    
A₁, A₂, X₁, X₂: category
L₁: A₁ ⟶ X₁
L₂: A₂ ⟶ X₂
FA: A₁ ⟶ A₂
FX: X₁ ⟶ X₂
α: FA ∙ L₂ ⟹ L₁ ∙ FX
twosided_disp_functor_comp_law FA FA
  (twosided_disp_cat_of_struct_cospans L₁)
  (twosided_disp_cat_of_struct_cospans L₂)
  twosided_disp_cat_of_struct_cospans_functor_data
 
A₁, A₂, X₁, X₂: category
L₁: A₁ ⟶ X₁
L₂: A₂ ⟶ X₂
FA: A₁ ⟶ A₂
FX: X₁ ⟶ X₂
α: FA ∙ L₂ ⟹ L₁ ∙ FX
x₁, x₂, x₃, y₁, y₂, y₃: A₁
xy₁: twosided_disp_cat_of_struct_cospans L₁ x₁ y₁
xy₂: twosided_disp_cat_of_struct_cospans L₁ x₂ y₂
xy₃: twosided_disp_cat_of_struct_cospans L₁ x₃ y₃
f₁: A₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
g₁: A₁ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧
fg₁: xy₁ -->[ f₁ ][ g₁] xy₂
f₂: A₁ ⟦ x₂, x₃ ⟧
g₂: A₁ ⟦ y₂, y₃ ⟧
fg₂: xy₂ -->[ f₂ ][ g₂] xy₃
(#2 twosided_disp_cat_of_struct_cospans_functor_data)
  (fg₁ ;;2 fg₂) =
trb₂ ((#2 twosided_disp_cat_of_struct_cospans_functor_data)
        fg₁ ;;2 (#2 twosided_disp_cat_of_struct_cospans_functor_data)
                  fg₂)

      
A₁, A₂, X₁, X₂: category
L₁: A₁ ⟶ X₁
L₂: A₂ ⟶ X₂
FA: A₁ ⟶ A₂
FX: X₁ ⟶ X₂
α: FA ∙ L₂ ⟹ L₁ ∙ FX
x₁, x₂, x₃, y₁, y₂, y₃: A₁
xy₁: twosided_disp_cat_of_struct_cospans L₁ x₁ y₁
xy₂: twosided_disp_cat_of_struct_cospans L₁ x₂ y₂
xy₃: twosided_disp_cat_of_struct_cospans L₁ x₃ y₃
f₁: A₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
g₁: A₁ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧
fg₁: xy₁ -->[ f₁ ][ g₁] xy₂
f₂: A₁ ⟦ x₂, x₃ ⟧
g₂: A₁ ⟦ y₂, y₃ ⟧
fg₂: xy₂ -->[ f₂ ][ g₂] xy₃
struct_cospan_sqr_ob_mor L₂
  ((#2 twosided_disp_cat_of_struct_cospans_functor_data)
     (fg₁ ;;2 fg₂)) =
struct_cospan_sqr_ob_mor L₂
  (trb₂ ((#2 twosided_disp_cat_of_struct_cospans_functor_data)
           fg₁ ;;2 (#2 twosided_disp_cat_of_struct_cospans_functor_data)
                     fg₂))

      
A₁, A₂, X₁, X₂: category
L₁: A₁ ⟶ X₁
L₂: A₂ ⟶ X₂
FA: A₁ ⟶ A₂
FX: X₁ ⟶ X₂
α: FA ∙ L₂ ⟹ L₁ ∙ FX
x₁, x₂, x₃, y₁, y₂, y₃: A₁
xy₁: twosided_disp_cat_of_struct_cospans L₁ x₁ y₁
xy₂: twosided_disp_cat_of_struct_cospans L₁ x₂ y₂
xy₃: twosided_disp_cat_of_struct_cospans L₁ x₃ y₃
f₁: A₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
g₁: A₁ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧
fg₁: xy₁ -->[ f₁ ][ g₁] xy₂
f₂: A₁ ⟦ x₂, x₃ ⟧
g₂: A₁ ⟦ y₂, y₃ ⟧
fg₂: xy₂ -->[ f₂ ][ g₂] xy₃
# FX (pr1 fg₁ · pr1 fg₂) =
# FX (struct_cospan_sqr_ob_mor L₁ fg₁)
· # FX (struct_cospan_sqr_ob_mor L₁ fg₂)

      apply functor_comp.
  Qed.

  
A₁, A₂, X₁, X₂: category
L₁: A₁ ⟶ X₁
L₂: A₂ ⟶ X₂
FA: A₁ ⟶ A₂
FX: X₁ ⟶ X₂
α: FA ∙ L₂ ⟹ L₁ ∙ FX
twosided_disp_functor FA FA
  (twosided_disp_cat_of_struct_cospans L₁)
